***нанять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нанять.html>наня́ть</a> (7478)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ня́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-njátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нанять.html>наня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nanjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нанимать.html>нанима́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hire, to engage</li>
<li>to rent, to lodge</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нанима́тель</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nanimátelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">наём</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">najóm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нанять.html>наня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nanjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наняться.html>наня́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nanjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наниматься.html>нанима́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get a job, to get hired</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нанять.html>наня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nanjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Colloquial pronunciation often puts the stress on the prefix in the past masculine, neuter, and plural, i.e. <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наняться.html>на́нялся</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:наняться.html>на́нялось</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:наняться.html>на́нялись</a></span>.</li></ul>

***наоборот.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наоборот.html>наоборо́т</a> (1181)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оборот.html>оборо́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oborót</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наоборот.html>наоборо́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naoborót</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>inside out, back to front</li>
<li>vice versa, the other way round, conversely</li>
<li>on the contrary, to the contrary</li></ol>
<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;">нареч.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:обратный.html>обра́тной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:противоположный.html>противополо́жной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>стороно́й</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обратный.html>обра́тной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:противоположный.html>противополо́жной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>стороны</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:надеть.html>Наде́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фуражка.html>фура́жку</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:наоборот.html>наоборо́т</a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:козырек.html>козырько́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:назад.html>наза́д</a>. </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:надеть.html>Наде́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубаха.html>руба́ху</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:наоборот.html>наоборо́т</a></span>. </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>Чита́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наоборот.html>наоборо́т</a>. </span></li>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрез.html>отре́з</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otréz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, known since the 18th century.

***нападать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нападать.html>напада́ть</a> (5175)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нападать.html>напада́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napadátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напасть.html>напа́сть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to attack, to fall on, to assault, to descend <i>(on)</i></li>
<li>to come across, to come upon, to hit on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:напасть.html>напа́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мысль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja napál na myslʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the thought occurred me</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(feeling, condition)</i> to come <i>(over)</i>, to grip, to seize, to overcome</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нападение.html>нападе́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">napadénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нападать.html>напа́дать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napádatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to fall <i>(some quantity)</i></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нападать.html>напада́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napadájuščij</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нападающий.html>напада́ющего</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нападающий.html>напада́ющие</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нападающий.html>напада́ющих</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нападающий.html>напада́ющая</a></b>)

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> forward

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">напа́д-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">napád-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***напасть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:напасть.html>напа́сть</a> (7770)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pastʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напасть.html>напа́сть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napástʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напасть.html>напа́сти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напасть.html>напа́сти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напасть.html>напа́стей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>misfortune, bad luck, trouble</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напасть.html>напа́сть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napástʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нападать.html>напада́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to attack, to fall on, to assault, to descend <i>(on)</i></li>
<li>to come across, to come upon, to hit on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:напасть.html>напа́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мысль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja <b>napál</b> na myslʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the thought occurred to me</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(feeling, condition)</i> to come <i>(over)</i>, to grip, to seize, to overcome</li></ol>

***напевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:напевать.html>напева́ть</a> (7678)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напеть.html>напе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">napétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напевать.html>напева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напеть.html>напе́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hum <i>(a melody)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sing <i>(demonstrating a melody)</i></li>
<li>to have one's singing recorded <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:напевать.html>напева́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:диск.html>диск</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>napevátʹ</b> disk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to record a disk (of one's singing)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to slander</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">hum</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мурлыкать.html>мурлы́кать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">murlýkatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">sing</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петь.html>петь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">petʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">record</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:записывать.html>запи́сывать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zapísyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">slander</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наговаривать.html>нагова́ривать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nagovárivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***напечатавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:напечатать.html>напеча́тавший</a> (3859)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напечатать.html>напеча́тавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napečátavšij</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:напечатать.html>напеча́тать</a> (3859)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печатать.html>печа́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pečátatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напечатать.html>напеча́тать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napečátatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печатать.html>печа́тать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to print <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to copy something on a surface, especially by machine</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to type <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to use a typewriter or to enter text or commands into a computer using a keyboard</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***напиваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:напиваться.html>напива́ться</a> (14626)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напиться.html>напи́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">napítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напиваться.html>напива́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napivátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напиться.html>напи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to quench thirst</li>
<li>to get drunk
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почему.html>почему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>лю́ди</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:напиваться.html>напива́ются</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́гут</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пить</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Počemú ljúdi <b>napivájutsja</b>, jésli ne mógut pitʹ?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Why do people get drunk, if they can't drink?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***напильник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>напильник</a> (23142)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Apparently from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">напили́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">napilítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, but the verb "to file" is actually <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">опили́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">opilítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>напи́льник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napílʹnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напильник.html>напи́льника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напильник.html>напи́льники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напильник.html>напи́льников</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>file, rasp <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">tool</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***напирать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:напирать.html>напира́ть</a> (12614)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-пира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-pirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напирать.html>напира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">напере́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to press</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to press, to push</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to emphasize, to give emphasis <i>(to)</i>, to point up</li></ol>
